2019-01-21 14:37:55,214 [11] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-21 14:37:57,536 [11] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC

2019-01-21 14:39:01,945 [9] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-21 14:39:21,426 [12] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'

2019-01-21 14:39:46,006 [11] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService.GetErrBinNo
SELECT T.*,
              CASE WHEN T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = 'E' THEN '空出库'
                   WHEN T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = 'P' THEN '先入品'
                   WHEN T.BIN_STATUS != '_' AND T1.PACKAGE_GUID IS NULL THEN '库位有货,库存无记录'
                   WHEN T.BIN_STATUS = '_' AND T1.PACKAGE_GUID IS NOT NULL THEN '库位无货,库存有信息'
                   WHEN T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = 'I' THEN '入库占用异常'
                   WHEN T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = 'O' THEN '出库占用异常'
               END ERR_NAME
              FROM PSB_BIN_STATUS T
              LEFT JOIN WBS_BIN T1
                ON T1.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
             WHERE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS IN ('E','P')
                OR (T.BIN_STATUS != '_' AND T1.PACKAGE_GUID IS NULL)
                OR (T.BIN_STATUS = '_' AND T1.PACKAGE_GUID IS NOT NULL)
                OR (T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS IN ('I','O') AND NOT EXISTS 
                   (SELECT 1 FROM WBS_TASK F WHERE F.SLOC_NO = T.BIN_NO OR F.ELOC_NO =  T.BIN_NO))
参数：

2019-01-21 14:43:49,720 [13] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2019-01-21 14:45:09,775 [17] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@SearchBinMaterial
SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO
参数：
@param0=2018/1/20 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/21 0:00:00

2019-01-21 14:45:25,279 [13] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T1.MATER_NO) MATER_NAME,
               SUM(1) BIN_COUNT,
                @param0  as BTIME,
              (1+ @param1 ) as ETIME
          FROM WBS_BIN T
          JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
         WHERE T2.USED_FLAG = 1
           AND T2.BIN_STATUS = CHAR(36)
           AND T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = '_'
        AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE >= @param0    AND  T1.PRODUCT_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
      GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
      ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO

2019-01-21 14:47:21,921 [13] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

      SELECT T.CRN_FORK_NO,T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE,T1.*,
             CASE T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_FORK_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_IN_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_IN_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_OUT_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_OUT_ENABLE_DESC
        FROM PSB_CRN_FORK T
        JOIN PSB_CRN T1 
          ON T1.CRN_NO = T.CRN_NO

      SELECT T.CRN_FORK_NO,T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE,T1.*,
             CASE T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_FORK_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_IN_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_IN_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_OUT_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_OUT_ENABLE_DESC
        FROM PSB_CRN_FORK T
        JOIN PSB_CRN T1 
          ON T1.CRN_NO = T.CRN_NO

      SELECT T.CRN_FORK_NO,T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE,T1.*,
             CASE T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_FORK_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_IN_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_IN_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_OUT_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_OUT_ENABLE_DESC
        FROM PSB_CRN_FORK T
        JOIN PSB_CRN T1 
          ON T1.CRN_NO = T.CRN_NO
